
1a1(ta): / 'dus pa rin po che'i rgyud dri ma med pa gzi brjid rab tu 'bar ba'i modo las bla med go 'pang thar lam bsgrub thabs kyi md bzhugs so// // 
1b1(ta): g.yung drung lha'i skad du na/
2a1(ta): a dkar khri sangs mu lam gsal/ gang zag mi yi skad du na/ bla med go 'phang
2a2(ta): thar lam bsgrub thabs kyi don bstan pa'i mdo/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa sprul pa'i sku
2a3(ta): la phyag 'tshal lo// de'i thse de'i dus na/ ston pa rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa sprul pa'i sku
2b1(ta): des/ 'gro basems can gyi don la dgongs nas/ mi mdzed kyi 'jig rten lhe 'dzam bu glang gi dmig/ sog kha bon gyi 'byung gnas/ gnas mchog dam pa 'ol mo glang chen / 
2b2(ta): gyi/ rgyal s po brang gling brgyad du sku 'khrungs nas/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi don mthar phyin par mdzad pa yi/ bstan pa rjes su bzhag par mdzad pa'i dus su / gnas mchog 
2b3(ta): dam pa 'ol mo gling chen gyi byang phyogs/ nang gi gling chen bcu gnyis kyi phyi rol/ ri bo snya mchog mdzes ri'i rtsa ba/ chu bo chen po pagzhu'i 'gram/ byang phyogs dmangs rigs 
2b4(ta): gdol pa'i gling / grong khyer chen po sproes ldan gyi dbus/ sku mkhar ba le bang so' nang na/ yab dmangs rigs kyi rgyal po khri brtan har dang / sum bram ze' btsun mo 'gu lang 
2b5(ta): b+un dha ma gnyis las/ sras lam dral gnyis blams te/ rgyal bu khri skying don bzang dang / bu mo khri btsun ting mdzes dang gnyis yod d/ rgyal 'khor dang longs spyod mnga'thang 
2b6(ta): shin tu mang zhing dpag tu med par yod do// de nas yang de'i tshe/ rgyal bu khri skyong don bzang ni/ shin tu yang mi rgyal brgyud ma'i bu / rig pa che zhing dbang po gsal ba/ shes pa dangs 
3a1(ta): / dran pa myur ba/ blo 'khrul che ga/ bsam pa btan pa/ rab tu gnas pa/ tshad la 'das pa zhig yod// de la gtsug rje rgyal po' bla mo/ gtsug tham ta/ 
3a2(ta): lo ma bya ba khab tu bzhes nas stang dang dbyal du tshogs te/ de la yang yab mas gzhan las kyang bsod nams dang longs spyod ldan zhing / phun sum tshogs pa'i dge rtags 'phel / 
3a3(ta): nas bbra shes pa dang ldan te/ dpal 'byor phun sum tshigs shing / sras khe'u gsum bu mo gnyis dang lnga ru bltams so// nor la yul de'i byang phyogs gnod sbyin nor gyi glang na/ 
3a4(ta): nor gyi lha pa d+ya re man ta'i dngos grub babs te/ yul de'i zangs brag lha rtsi'i nges nas rin po che'i gter mdzod rdol ba dang / 'dun s kun dga' ra ba'i phyi rol tu/ dpag 
3a5(ta): bsam pan n s+dzon pa'i tshal rgyas pa dang / gseng bar na bar me tog gi s+dzongs la/ na lug gnag gsum rkang 'gros kyi yo 'khyel ba dang / 'chags mdonhad sntar ma'i s+dzongs 
3a6(ta): la/ 'bru dgu lo tog bang mdzod kyi bcud smin pa dang / gzhan yang rgyal khams dang mnga' ras gzhan las dpag pa ra/ kun gyis che basbyin pa dang / zhal blta ba dang / lo 
3b1(ta): mtchod dang / zla dus dang / gnas skabs su bkur ste dang / rim gro phun sum tshogs pa ru byed do// de nas de'i tshe/ dus res shig na/ dbyar zla ba chung gi ches bco lnga la/ rgyal bu de 
3b2(ta): sku mkhar gyi bad la gzims nas bzhugs te/ tho rangs tsam na bsnyel gzim pa'i rmaM lam la/ mdun gyi bar snang la/ bud med dar dkar gyi ral ga la/ dar dmar gyi yang / 
3b3(ta): sham brgyan pa zhig gis/ phyag na zla ba nya gang ba 'dra ba'i man 'dal dbyibs legs pa gcig la/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che zhig gis rgyan bkram nas/ spyan gyis 
3b4(ta): rgyal bu la gzigs shing tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ gang dag srid pa gsum po na/ mnga' dbang rgyal por gyur pa'i mi/ dbang la dbang bya ma brgyan na/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor ma 
3b5(ta): mthong zhing / yid bzhin nor bu ma 'chang na/ dbang sgyur dmangs dang ci ma 'dra/ gang dag sal par gyur pa'i mi/ 'jig rten skyed kho s nam la/ brtson 'grus rtsol bsdrag 
3b6(ta): gzhan gyis/ bsod nams phal cher de dang 'dra/ 'jig rten 'di bden snang ba la/ lo gis nor phyir ma gtogs par/ phyi ma yid bzhin nor 'chang na/ rtag par phun tshogs srid 
4a1(ta): / pa tsam/ rgyal bu dam pa khri skying bzang / da ltha dal 'byor mi lus kyi/ dbang chen rgyal bur skyes pa'i tshe/ dbang sgyur rang dbang btsan pa la/ gzhan dbang dag gi lhad / 
4a2(ta): med pas/ zla ba nya ba'i dkyil 'khor 'dzin/ yid bzhin nor bu bye dor gyis/ phal pa'i dmangs las gongsar 'phags/ gang dag rien chen der 'dzin par/ de ya yon tan 'thob 
4a3(ta): par 'gyur/ zhes zer nas mi snang ba gyur to// de la rgyal bu des/ phyi nangs nam langs pa'i dang po/ nyi ma shar ba'i rtsi mo la/ sku mkhar gyi rtse la byin nas dpyad btang bas/ 
4a4(ta): mdangs gsum gyi rmaM lam dang brda thabs de rnams ni/ 'di lta ba ru 'dug ste/ bud med dkar mo ni/ ye shes dbyings kyi dbal mo 'gro ba'i don du byin nas bdag la lung bstan par 
4a5(ta): rigs so// zla ba nya gang ba'i dkyil 'khor ni/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad kyi nang nas bstan pa rjes bhag rnam par rgyal ba'i mdzad pa la zer bar rigs so// yid 
4a6(ta): bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che ni sangs rgyas bstan pa'i gtso bo ston pa gnhen rab mi bo yi/ sku la bkur ste dang rim gro cher byas na/ 'di dang phyi ma gnyis ka'i don thams cad / 
4b1(ta): yongs su ma btsal lhun gyis grub pa ru 'grub ces bya ba rnu rigs so// phal pa'i dmangs las gong sar 'phags zhes bya ba ni/ mnga' dbang gi rgyal por skyes kyang / las dge ba 
4b2(ta): la ma spyod na/ 'jig rten 'di' bsod nams dang longs spyod ci yod kyang / phal pa'i dmangs las ma dpag cing / dbang ldan gyi rgyal po ru skyes pa'i dus su/ gzhan dbang log 
4b3(ta): pa'i phyogs su ma gol bar/ rang dbang dge ba'i las la spyod na/ rgyal po gzhan dang mi 'dra ba/ kun gyi nang nas bsod nams dang longs spyod/ gzhan las khyad par du 'phags 
4b4(ta): zhes bya bar rigs so// des na rgyal bu des/ phyi de nam gyi tho rings nas/ rgyal khams dang mnga' 'bangs rnams la sbran btang nas/ rgyal blon thams cad rin po che'i rgyal sar 
4b5(ta): kun tshogs nas rgyal bus bka' stsal pa/ gsoen dang rgyal po yab yum blon 'bangs rnams/ 'o skol rgyal sa dam par skyes nas kyang / 'khor los sgyur rgyal rang dbang thob / 
4b6(ta): dus 'dir/ 'di phyi gnyis ka'i don zhig ma bsgrub cing / dkar po dge ba'i las shig ma spyad na/ dbang bsgyur rgyal por skyes pa ci la phan/ bsod nams longs spyod phun sum ci 
5a1(ta): tshigs kyang / gnan dag pal pa dmangs dang ci ma 'a/ dbang chen rgyal la dbang byas ma brgyan na/ 'jig rten 'di bden mi che dmangs yang skyed/ 'di pbye gnyis su 
5a2(ta): phan pa'i dbang sgyur gyis/ dkar po dge ba'i las zhig ma spyod na/ lho gs nor gyi rtsol ba damangs yang mkhas/ sangs rgyas bstan pa'i lam la ma zhugs na/ log bslu 'khor / 
5a3(ta): ba'i rjes 'brang kun ka yin/ bla med thar pa'i 'bras bu ma bsgrub na/ ngan song dmyal ba'i 'gram rdo gang yang 'gro/ de phyir gzhan dag gang las dpag pa yi/ de rang 'di pyi gnyis 
5a4(ta): ka'i don yod phyir/ dkar po dge ba'i las shig bgyi bar 'thad/ dge ba'i las la rnam pa gnyis yin te/ rgya chen spyod dang kor cer bsgrub pa gnyis/ rgya cher spyod pa dge ba 
5a5(ta): gzhan don dang / kor cer bsgrub pa rang don gnyis yin te/ de gnyis rgya mtsho ba glang cig rjes chu/ nam mkha'i dbyings dang gsal mthongs skar dang mtshungs/ de phyir gnan las 
5a6(ta): stobs su dpag pa dang // de rang rgyal 'khor sgrib sbyangs tshogs s+dzogs dang / phyi rabs 'gro ba gzhan la phan pa'i phyir/ gnas mchog dam pa rgyal s chen po nas/ ston pa'i sgron / 
5b1(ta): ma gnhen rab spyan drang zhing / bla med thar lam bsgrub pa'i bon cig zhu/ phyei rabs rnams la bstan pa'i dpe ru bzhag/ rgyal khams mnga' res dge ba'i las la bcud/ 'di dang 
5b2(ta): phyi ma gnyis kar don yod bya/ zhes rgyal bus smras nas mchad gleng pas de la rgyal po yab kyis smras pa/ gsen dang rgyal po blon 'khor srgas sum rnams/ rgyal bus smras pa'i 
5b3(ta): tshig la rjes yi rang / bdag kyang de lazhin tu mngon par 'dud/ rgyal po'i las spyod khrims dang rna yin kyang / phyi ma'i md don ster na bdud kyi las/ rang mhe dregs pa ldan pas ci / 
5b4(ta): la pan/ 'khor g.yog na gzhung nag po bdud kyang bzang / bu la na tsha na zan drin kyang che/ de phyir 'jig rten 'di bden ma gtogs par/ phyi mar ngan song gnas brgyud 'khor 
5b5(ta): bar 'khyams/ de pyir bdu sren bu dang tci ma khyad/ 'jig rten 'di ru yo byad ci tshogs kyang / me rtag sgyu ma'i rgyu bsam re re yin/ 'jig rten 'di ru dbang chen ci tshogs kyang / 
5b6(ta): skad cig phyi ma dran pa srid pa tsam/ rgyal bu khyed ni gzhan dang mi 'dra bar/ yab mes gong ma rnams las dpag pa che/ 'byor ldan yo byad bcu 'gyur tsam du 'phel/ da yang phyi / 
6a1(ta): ma'i don zhig bsam nas su/ rgyal 'khor mag 'sres dge bar bkol ba dang / sangs rgyas bstan pa rjes du 'dzin pa dang / phye rabs rnams la dpe dang don bstan na/ 
6a2(ta): ston pa'i phron ma myur bar spyan rngs zhig/ dge la byi bshol le los bar du gcod/ dpyer bsam pas brtson 'grus rab tu gyur/ gyur la tang tshod gyur du 'grub ste mtshi
6a3(ta): zhes bka' stsal pas/ btsun mo dang / blon po dang / de dpon dang / 'khor rnams kyang zhin tu yang spro b skyes nas/ rgyal po yab sras bka' la nyan zhing / dge ba'i las la 
6a4(ta): thang gcad par gros kyis bcad do// de nas yang de'i tshe/ rgyal bu de ston pa'i sgron ma spyan 'dren du chas te/ de yang 'khor du gtogs pa'i blon po dang / ded dpon dang / dmag mi stong 
6a5(ta): gis 'khor dang chas nas rol mo'i tshogs mang po dang bcas te/ de yang rgyal bu nyid ni sku la za 'og bar khyim gyi bar chen ni gsol/ dbu la le brgan dmar po'i 'gying thod ni 
6a6(ta): bcings/ glo la gnam lcags 'bar ba'i ya tsa ni btags/ phyag na sba dkar 'phrul gyi 'gying kar ni bsnams nas/ gyi ling sngon po g.yu srog la bcibs nas phyi blon dang / nang 
6b1(ta): blon dang / b slon dang / de dpon dang / bran 'khor dang / po tye dang / sgra mcan dng / rig khyed dng / sku gzhein dang bcas na phyogs bsher da chen pbon pbyar te/ rchu b pag 
6b2(ta): zlu'i rgyud nas kha lho phyogs su bstan te ston pa'i sgron ma spyan 'drin du ghegs so// de nas de'i tshe/ yul de' nang rol gyi byang phyogs gnod sbyin nor gling gi phyi rol/ lthagsar 
6b3(ta): chen po'i rgyab/ rgya mtshoe n tra 'khyil chen gyi dkyil/ shing a par ldon pa'i tshal dang / 'dam bu ne'u gsing gi ldang rnams 'khrungs nas/ shin tu lam ma byed par gyur nas/ 
6b4(ta): zhag dang zla ba mang por 'gor bar gyur te// gzhan yang nyin mo rgya mtsho chu glang dang / nags tshal lam rang du byed kyang / tnhub mo sha za dang / 'byung po dang / mi ma yin gyi dmag 
6b5(ta): tshogs mang pos bskor nas shin tu 'jigs pa dang / yang ba dang / bag tsha bar gyur nas/ nyon mongs pa dang / nyam thag pa'i sdug bsngal mang po nyams su myong bar byungngo// de la / 
6b6(ta): rgyal bu des/ de mod srid la 'byung ba'i lha dang / bde bar gshegs pa la mchod pa'i bye brag mang po bshams nas spul te gsol ba btab pa/ na mo dbyings na bzhugs pa'i dus 
7a1(ta): gsum bde bar gshegs/ sngon dang ma'ongs da ltadus gsum gyi/ 'das dang bkhyon phyogs bcu' rgyal ras dang / 'drul gtson dng gsung du sems dpa' rnams/ dus / 
7a2(ta): 'dir bdag la gsen cing dgongs su gsol/ dngos 'byor yid sprul bla med mchod pa'i tshogs/ bdag gi lus ngag gus pas bshams pa 'di/ rgyal ba sras bcas tshogs la mchod 
7a3(ta): pa 'brul/ thugs rjes byin gyis rlobs la bzhes su gsol/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can thams cad kyi/ byang chub bsgrub la bar chad med pa dang / bsam don dge ba mthar 
7a4(ta): phyin mdzad du gsol/ bder gshegs dbyings na bzhugs pa'i gsal bar mkhyen/ ston pa'i sgron ma skyabs mgon 'dren pa'i dpal/ bdag cag thugs rjes gsal bar mi 
7a5(ta): dgongs na/ 'dren pa'i thugs rje nye rang yid dam ci/ 'gro ba ma nus nyam thag gdungs pa yi/ rmongs shing lcugs pa'i sdug bsngal bskyab tu gsol/ zhes hin tu gdung ba'i dbyangs 
7a6(ta): kyis gsol ba btab pas/ de su'i thugs su dgongs shing snyan du byin na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa gshen rab nyid kyi/ thugs su dgongs shing snyan du byin nas/ thugs 
7b1(ta): las sprul pa'i 'odi zer grangs med par spres nas/ byang phyogs su bkyes pa'i/ rgyal bu gtso 'khor rnams kyi mdun gyi nam mkha' la/ nye ma'i dkyil 'khor rab tu rgyas te mun 
7b2(ta): pa'i shag rnam bsal nas/ bar snang la sprul pa'i lha dmag bye ba sa ya grangs med par byung nas/ bdud dang sren po dang mu stegs la sogs te/ dge ba la bar chad byed pa'i tshogs 
7b3(ta): rnams byer zhing dnges par gyur to// de la rgyal bu gtso 'khor rnams/ shin tu bag dro ba dang ngal ba seMs par gyur nas/ bde bar gshegs pa la gsol ba btab pa la/ shin tu yang / 
7b4(ta): dang spro ba dang dga' ba skyes so// de nas yang nangs par nam langs kyi tho rangs la/ nam mkha' la gzugs med pa'i sgra snyan pa zhig grags pa las/ rgyal po dam pa khri snying re// 
7b5(ta): dge la bar chad med pa dang / 'jigs pa brgyad las skyobs pa yi/ gsang ba'i gzungs sngags bdag gis bshad/ ma yeings dbang po brnyan par nyon/ phyir na dad ldan dam tshig can/ 
7b6(ta): gang gis mi sgyur bcos mi bslud/ dge ba'i las la 'jug spyod nas/ lus srog gyur kyang bzod thob na/ bzod pa bsran dang bcas pa yi/ brtson 'grus myur gyis gzhu bdungs 
8a1(ta): nas/ bsam gtan rgyud la lhod med kyi/ shes rab mgyogs pa'i mda' 'pangs na/ bskal drid 'byung ba 'khrugs gyur yang / dge la bar chad 'byung ma 'gyur/ de 
8a2(ta): lta blo thag mchod kyis/ rang nyid mdun ma rang gis gcod/ rang sems 'gyur med gasng ldan la/ gzhan dbang rkyen gyis ga la 'jig/ de phyir rang sems dpang btsugs gcis/ 
8a3(ta): 'on kyang don dam kun s+dzob gnyis/ zung 'brel bden gnyis ldan pa'i phyir/ lam gyi gnod pas mi tshugs zhing / dge la bar chad mi 'byung phyer/ gsang ba'i gzungs mchog 
8a4(ta): bdag gis bshad/ A+o~M na ma a dkar ha ra mu lam gsal 'bar/ mu ye khri dkar sa mun ta/ sad la ha ra smi ta ma ma shud raM ya/ kr ta kro ta nye lo yo a ma dha na ra ri/ sa / 
8a5(ta): ma ya ma hA yagag bas ste b+ho s ma ya lo ka baM ta/ me d sangs gsal har/ ko ta ka te/ b+han dha b+han dha/ r+ha ba k ta na shan ta bha ta ha ba dad de/ pra ti ti ste rad na ni/ lo / 
8a6(ta): skas tba 'dza te/ a rgam me ta pa tra/ sniM gyad sad de ha ra htasr/ zhu lo zhu lo/ tsan tra zhu lo/ sad+yu na ma pa r+ya bra can/ b+han dha hi ya ho yangsa ma yanghA de ltar gsang 
8b1(ta): ba'i gzungs mcshog 'di/ dar dkar dag la bris nas su/ mi thub rgyal mtshan rtser sbyar na/ ci bsam don rnams 'grub pa dang / lam gyi 'jigs pa mi 'byung zhing / dge ba'i / 
8b2(ta): las rnams mthar bhyin 'gyur/ skyes bu dam pa rdul zhugs can/ dge ba'i las la cang bcad cing / blo gros phun tshogs dbang phyug rgyal/ dge la dad mos 'dun spyod pa/ bskal / 
8b3(ta): par 'gyur med rin chen gser/ dad pa drag po phyir mi ldog/ brtson 'gruns drag po yun mi brtsi/ sangs rgyas dung phyin zhal mdal te/ ci bsam don kun myur 'grub 'gyur/ 
8b4(ta): zhes zer ba'i sgra skad dang / lung bstan par byungngo// de'i phyir nangs par nam langs pa'i dang po/ nyi m shar ba'i rtsi mo la/ rgyal bu yang shin tu dang spro ba dang mngon par dga' nas/ 
8b5(ta): yang bde bar gshegs pa la 'byu dang / rin po che dang / bdud rtsi pud kyis mchod pas/ yul de'i mtsho glang dang / nags tshal gyi s+dzongs la/ sngana ma mthong ba'i lam gcig lho 
8b6(ta): phyogs su rnyed nas 'dug go/ de ltar gzungs de dar dkar la bris nas/ rgyal mtshan gyi rtsi la btags nas phyogs bzhi ru phyar nas/ gzungs de nar mar 'don pa dang / kha ton du 
9a1(ta): / 'don pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / 'chang ba dang / klog par byed cing lam du zhugs nas song ba la/ dge ba'i bar chad thams cad nye bar zhe nas/ lam drangs pa dang / bul / 
9a2(ta): bde ba dang / bza' btang dang so byad 'phel ba la sogs te/ dge tags pun sum tshogs pa dang ldan no// de nas de' csho de'dus na/ ston pa gzen rab mo bo ni/ rgyal po rgyal 
9a3(ta): rigs kyi 'gro don mthar phyin nas/ sur 'ol mo gling chen du pebs te/ gsas mkhar khong ma one' chung gi nang na/ 'khor rnams la/ chab dkar drag po sngags kyi bon ston zheng 
9a4(ta): bzhugs na/ yul de'i byang phyogs/ pho brang chen po sgyu 'phrul dga' ba can gyi phyi rol/ me tog sna tshogs kyi gling la/ rol mo'i tshogs mang po 'ong nas 'dug go/ de nas grong 
9a5(ta): byer gyi phyi rol tu bhyin pa dang / mtshan dang ldan pa'i khye'u khyad par du dpag pa gcig la/ 'khor pa dmag mi 'khor tshogs stong gis bskor nas byungngo// grong khyer gyi mi rnams 
9a6(ta): kyis dris pas/ de rnams ni phyi rol gyi rgyalgs nas/ pho brang du dmu rigs kyi rgyal po la mzhal du 'ong ba yin pas/ da yang khyed rnams kyi shul mtshon la de rnams rgyal po la 
9b1(ta): mdzal 'tshal gyis/ zhes zer ro// grong khyer gyi ma rnams kyang rgyal s yang tsig tu sebs nas/ sten pa'i spyan pgar zhus pas sten pas zhal nas rigs kyi bra de rnams ni/ 'o 
9b2(ta): skol gyi byang phyogs na/ dmangs rigs kyi rgyal s chen po nas/ 'o skol la mdal du 'ong ba yin pas/ da yang g.sung du bon gyi bstan pa la gnas shing / bstan pa 'dzin pa'i 
9b3(ta): gnas su gyur pas/ khyed rnams kyi rol mo dang mdun nas bsdus la/ rgyal s yang tchig tu khrid la shog cig/ ces bka' ba rtsal to// der 'khor rnams kyis kyang / ston pas / 
9b4(ta): bka' stsal ba bzhin du rol mo'i tshogs dang bcas nas mdun nas bsdus te/ rgyal sa yang thog tu mchis nas ston pa dang zhal mzal lo// ston pas zhal nas gsungs pa/ 
9b5(ta): rigs kyi bu khyed rnams/ dmag ma dang rol mo'i dpung dang bcas nas/ yul gyi mng ni ji skad bya ba nas yin/ rigs ni gar gtogs/ pa dang ma la ni ci ming / bdag rang gi mang 
9b6(ta): ni ji skad bya ba lags/ gnas 'di ru 'ong ba ni don ched ci'i phyir 'ong ba lags/ zhes bka' stsal pas/ de la rgyal bu khri skyong gis/ s+dzas kyi nor bsrung shel las grub pa zur / 
10a1(ta): bcudug zhig nyen pal blal n / rton pa'i sgra b brtor bzhi bya/ b byagn 'bo'/ bchod zhi brul n nyon pa'i bduon ddung bcog thalbo/ 
10a2(ta): sbyar nas gsol pa/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa lags/ bdag cag mchaMs pa'i yul gyi ban zhi/ ro bo tya mtshog mzhes do'i rtsa ba/ cho b pagsu' 'gram/ 
10a3(ta): dmangs rigs gdol pa'i gling zhes bya ba lags so// grong khyer gyi ming ni spros ldan zhes bya ba lags so// sku mkhar gyi ming zhi ba le bang so bya ba lags so// rigs ni dmangs 
10a4(ta): rigs gdol pa'i rigs lags so// yab ni dmangs rigs kyi rgyal po khri brtyan ha ra bya ba lags so// yum ni bram ze' bu mo 'gu ling bhi te bya ba lags so// bdag rang gi 
10a5(ta): mang ni rgyal bu khri skyong don bzang bya ba lags so// gnas 'di ru mchis pa'i don ni d kyi yul do ni rgyal 'khor dang / bsod nams dang longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa ru yod kyang // 
10a6(ta): las dge ba byed pa la/ dge ba'i phyogs su mos shing cha tsam spyod par ma gtogs pa/ shin tu dge spyod ngo mtshar dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i stobs la 'dzug par med pas/ gnas 'di 
10b1(ta): dru sten pa'i phron ma spyan 'dren du mches pa lags'so// deyang ston pa'i phron ma 'gro ba'i dpal dang bzhin/ bdag gi.yul dang gnas der gshegs par bhu/ gsung du bon gyi / 
10b2(ta): bstan pa rjes bhag dang / rgyal khams mnga' ris dge la btcud pa dang / bdag cag bsam don 'grub par mdzad du gsol/ zhes gsol to// de la ston pas kyang thugs dgyes 
10b3(ta): par mdzad nas/ 'khor rnams la bka' stsal pa/ 'khor du gtogs pa'i gnhen rab g.yung dung sems dpa' rnams dang / rgyal s pho brang gling brgyad kyi ma rnams/ bdag ni 'gro
